<GmapID>0x808f9da258baf499:0x613d11daafbb9298<//GmapID>< Review>
In door outdoor dining. Food was delish. Mains were 18oz ribeye, Mary's Bistro Chicken, Brisket Pappardelle in creamy sauce, Skirt Steak. Meats were cook to perfection and flavorful. Appetizers: Mushroom Bruschetta and Calamari were absolutely delish. Fried Brussel Sprouts was ok. Beet salad was also very good. Can't find much wrong with Saltyard, give it a try. Note: not a cheap lunch so bring money. My meal, including tip and tax, $75.00. It was worth it. All health protocols were followed.< /Review>

< Review>
SO so so impressed by the food here!! My friend recommended it and I am so glad we got to try this place. Inside is definitely a more classy and modern feel. I came here around 7:30pm on a Tuesday and it was packed. A table left shortly after and we were seated immediately. We ordered the mixed greens salad and calamari first, and for entrees: filet mignon medallions, paella, and salmon.

The calamari and salad were great starters. They also give complimentary bread too. It did take a while for the entrees to come out, but we were enjoying eating and talking. When the food came out, it looked amazing. The salmon was well cooked and went well with the potatoes. The paella was super filling, but had such a great mix of seafood. The medallions was the best dish though; the filet mignon was SO tender. Each bite was amazing.

I would highly recommend this place. The food here is fresh and amazing. It would be a great place for a date with its modern and sleek decor. I would love to come here again soon.< /Review>

<Review>This truly was a 5-star Thanksgiving experience, which was a surprise because we booked at the last minute. Such a pleasant surprise! Easy parking right out front, and, better yet, amazing service from drinks through dessert. Wonderful, craft cocktails got us started off right. We had calamari and Brussels sprouts for apps, followed by rave-worth clam chowder and delightful tomato and burrata salad. Two in our party had fall-off-the-bone short ribs, one a traditional turkey dinner that was reportedly moist and delicious, with just the right balance of herb seasoning. The chef transformed a meat-centered pappardelle into an amazing veggie dish for me (though more veggie options on the mains menu would be nice). All of this bounty would have made for a wonderful dinner on its own, but the superlative service--attentive, but never pushy--resulted in a relaxed, enjoyable Thanksgiving dinner. <Review>I went for dinner this past Saturday and was pleasantly surprised. The restaurant took over the space from Ecco and redid the layout. I don't really think much was carried over the previous place, but that's not uncommon.

I started with the prosciutto flatbread appetizer and it was the weakest link. It was a great combo of ingredients, but the crust was a bit underdone for my liking. As the saying goes, "your mileage may differ".

My entree was a duck confit pasta dish which was superb. It had the right balance for me. And the menu is surprisingly varied. They had everything from Niman Ranch cheeseburgers to risotto.

Another element I liked was the acoustics. There are a number of great restaurants in town, but have terrible acoustics.  That's not the case here as you can hear the folks in your dinner party.  For reference,  I was in the back corner table.

The staff was attentive and courteous. They were also apologetic too as I initially wanted the cheeseburger, but there was a grill problem. The better news is that duck pasta was far better than a cheeseburger.

Bottom line is I would definitely go back.<//Review>< rate>
4</rate>

Short story: skip it.

We came in for dinner but after sharing a small plate or two we decided it wasn't worth staying for dinner.

Crab tacos - tastewise these were ok. The crab tasted fresh and it wasn't overpowered by the other ingredients. For $18, though, these tacos needed double the amount of crab in them.

Charred broccoli and sunchoke - this should have been called arugula salad. It was a small pile of arugula with three florets of blanched, not charred, broccoli and two small sunchoke chunks. This salad was beyond disappointing.

My cocktail was overly sweet and tasted like there was no alcohol in it. My boyfriend ordered a Jameson and soda and got a Jack Daniels, then a Jameson and coke, before the drink was right.

Our bill came to $50 for a frustrating experience. Not sure if they're still working through opening kinks or what, but I don't plan to go back.<//Review>

Waiter was profusely apologetic but manager chose to ignore the situation. That really soured my experience and I wrote a 1 star review though would have loved to give less for the service.

Some months later, the Manager Baris contacted me and apologized.  To make matters right he invited me back with a complimentary bottle of wine.  We returned and invited our friend from last time and her SFO.  Baris ended up not only giving us some nice wine, but also some delicious appetizers and deserts.  Not only that, I come to find out that my friend had been back another time recently.  The waiter recognized her from the spill event and also gave her a glass of wine on the house.

So despite some stumbles at the beginning, Baris and his team more than made up for a catastrophic experience.  As before, the food here is quite delicious.  The short rib pappardelle really stood out...as did the cheesecake at the end.

Old Review:   I‚Äôd give em 4 stars for the food.   4 stars for service in general but 0 Star for the owner/manager willing to do what‚Äôs right.

Three of us had drinks and a meal here.  Ordered three flights of drinks so 9 glasses.  Waiter brought them over and managed to spill and break 7 of them as he served them.   There was broken glass everywhere and a bunch of wine spilled on my pants shirt and jacket.

Of course I did not have anything to change into but stayed for dinner despite me being soaked in wine.  You can probably see where this is going but before I get there, I want to be fair about the food.

We had several pasta dishes including a short rib and everything was quite good.  Also had a piece of cheesecake for desert which was not bad.

So we get the bill and I would have thought even a small discount would have been appropriate given the circumstance.  But there was nothing.  My partner went to talk to the host who claimed to be the owner and after some discussion he took off one piece cake for the incident.  Mind you I‚Äôm still soaked at this point.

In any case, the host never said anything To me and by not addressing the bill showed that he could not have cared less.  Bottom line for me is that based on the owners lack of concern to try to make the situation right, I won‚Äôt be back and don‚Äôt recommend it.   There are too many exceptional restaurants in the area to bother with this one.</review>

< review>
Just stopped in to check this place out and was very impressed! The workers are young, but so friendly and helpful. I asked for drinks they would recommend and the worker helping me walked me through the menu and made it really easy for me to understand my options and to make a decision. Excellent customer service! Also, they serve boba, tea, and coffee here, so there're options for everyone. I tried the passion fruit juice w/ agar jelly and aloe vera, which is awesome if you like passion fruit (I would start out at 30% sugar though, just to be on the safe side. You can always add more sugar later!) I also got a cafe Americano, hot and black, since I was in need of some energy, and it was so yummy! The place itself is so clean and the style is very modern, yet warm and colorful. They have a lot of tables where people can come in and stay and chill for awhile, just like any other tea or coffee shop. They even have games set up for people to play. What a cool little boba/tea/coffee shop! I'm so glad such a chill place with yummy drinks has opened up in Modesto! (And they're open til 10 pm, which is hard to find for a shop like this locally. Yay!)< /review>

<username>IAN WENTZ< /username>< review>
I have been having my boat and pwc serviced here for the past 5 years and have nothing but great things to say about Lake Elsinore Marine.  They have always gone the extra mile to make sure our boat was in great shape for the summer.  There is definitely a reason why they are so busy- because they honest, knowledgeable and friendly.  They offer a great selection of parts and accessories, their store has saved our weekend a few times.  All of the mechanics are very knowledgeable and the girls in the office are a blast and know their boats.  Last summer they replaced the engine in our Larson, their price was unbeatable and the quality of work was unmatched.  The final bill was less than the estimate I was given and the work was done in a very timely manner.  We could not have been more pleased.  They are normally booked about 10-14 days out so you will have to wait for your boat to be worked on but it is well worth your wait.  Like I said prior- there is a reason why they are so busy- its because they are very good at what they do.< /review>

< review>
RUN don't walk away!!!!!! At first this seems like a nice place to bring your boat but its not. My problem started last year around august of 2012. I took my 89 bayliner capri with a l-drive to the shop to have my carbs synchronize after I cleaned them and my timing checked. I spoke with the owner and explained that this engine is not for the novice they are very picky he told my he would have his best mechanic Linsy on it so I was satisfied. Then after a week of no calls I decided to check in. I was then told a kid named Oscar was working on the boat :(. So I talked to him and he said great news the boat was running.(IT ALREADY RAN) I explained to him that it didn't have a problem running. He then said the stator was on to tight and he had to take off the fly wheel to fix it so I ok the repair. #weeks go by before I call back. He says he is having trouble getting it to time and asked if it ran fine before :(  which it did. He then said Linsy  was going to have to work on it :(. I finally get a call Dec 2,2012 Linsy said he doesn't know why it wont time but he was going to do a few more things to it. Finally I call April of 2013 and Linsy has given up told me to pick up my boat. No prob I said. When I went to pick up my boat it was covered :) but it had been sitting with all the spark plugs removed :(.... They had lost my transom saver which irreplaceable since they do not make them for my boat any more but I was told if I and I repeat I was to find one they would pay me back for it GRRRRRR. So when I got home to do the job my self Oscar had put the trigger back on backwards , Cracked my timing adjuster and lost the jam nut that hold the adjuster in place. AAAWWWWW  Which I was able to see in 5 minutes of inspection. So one day later and the cost of a timing gun I had my boat running and timed. Did I mention this is my first boat EVER. So I did the job of a boat repair tech with 37 years of experience in one day which he failed at doing with almost 9 months of trying.  Sorry for the long review but like I said Run away from this store since their appears to be no actual boat tech working there.</review>

< review>
I absolutely love this place!!! Not only is it clean, but the employees are super nice and greet you right away and if they are busy with another customer or what not they will let you know they'll be with you in a moment not like other places where they leave you standing there and not acknowledge you even being there... I am on my third visit here and it has been awesome since day one when i switched from Mommy's nutritional center in Azusa.

I had called ahead of time to ensure that they had the formula i was looking for, not only did they have it but when i walked in the person i spoke with recognized my voice and took her time to walk over and speak to me and say thank you for taking the time to check them out and all. And since I was a first timer there they took time to explain to me the process that they have : if your getting fruits and veggies you take a number and a basket and get your coupons worth amd then they'll call you up, if not you go straight to the person so they can get you your milk, cereal, formula, etc. It's a great place they have a good variety of fruits and vegetables they also have eggs, chorizo, guava, water and different types of drinks and snacks that i definitely did not see at Mommy's nutritional center at all. Not only were their attitudes positive they were just nice all around where as in the other place they look like they dont even want to be there at all lol. They also help you carry everything out to your car in a little shopping cart. They're also bilingual they speak English and Spanish. And are open early by 7:30 am which is also a nice thing unless your not a morning person.</review>
